<script type="text/javascript">
    window.onload = function () {
        const pageEnum = {
            'Select': 'select',
            'Itinerary': 'itinerary'
        };
        const queryParameter = {
            'utm_content': '&utm_content='
        };

        const perbookingCodesToAdd = ['SMS']

        const constants = {
            'decimals': 2
        };

        function getTotalFares(booking) {
            var totalFares = 0;
            booking.journeys.forEach(journey => {
                journey.fares.forEach(fare => {
                    totalFares += parseFloat(fare.totalAmount);
                })
            });
            return totalFares;
        }

        function shouldAddSSR(ssr) {
            return perbookingCodesToAdd.some(elem => elem === ssr);
        }

        function getTotalServices(booking) {
            var totalServices = 0;
            if (booking.pricing.breakdown.perPaxSegment != null && booking.pricing.breakdown.perPaxSegment != undefined) {
                booking.pricing.breakdown.perPaxSegment.forEach(service => {
                    totalServices += parseFloat(service.totalAmount);
                })
            }
            if (booking.pricing.breakdown.perBooking != null && booking.pricing.breakdown.perBooking != undefined) {
                booking.pricing.breakdown.perBooking.forEach(service => {
                    if (service.charges != null && service.charges != undefined) {
                        service.charges.forEach(charge => {
                            if (shouldAddSSR(charge.code)) {
                                totalServices += charge.amount;
                            }
                        })
                    }
                })
            }
            if (booking.pricing.breakdown.perPax != null && booking.pricing.breakdown.perPax != undefined) {
                booking.pricing.breakdown.perPax.forEach(service => {
                    totalServices += parseFloat(service.totalAmount);
                })
            }
            return totalServices;
        }
        var marketInSession = sessionStorage.getItem('marker');
        var thereIsmarketInSession = marketInSession != '' && marketInSession != null;
        var url = location.href;
        var queryHasParameter = url.includes(queryParameter.utm_content);
        if (url.includes(pageEnum.Select) && queryHasParameter) {
            var startIndex = url.indexOf(queryParameter.utm_content);
            if (startIndex != -1) {
                if (!queryHasParameter && thereIsmarketInSession) {
                    sessionStorage.removeItem('marker')
                } else {
                    var query = url.substring(startIndex).replace(queryParameter.utm_content, '');
                    var endIndex = query.indexOf('&');
                    parameterValue = query.substring(0, endIndex);
                    sessionStorage.setItem('marker', parameterValue);
                }
            }
        }
        if (url.includes(pageEnum.Itinerary) && thereIsmarketInSession) {
            var booking = JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.getItem("DP-sessionData"))._value.session.booking;
            var pixel = document.getElementById('TrackerAviasales');
            var pnr = booking.bookingInfo.recordLocator;
            var currencySymbol = booking.pricing.currency;
            var totalFares = getTotalFares(booking).toFixed(constants.decimals);
            var totalServices = getTotalServices(booking).toFixed(constants.decimals);
            marketInSession = sessionStorage.getItem('marker');
            var linkSource = 'https://pixel.aviasales.ru/pobeda?CurrencySymbol=' + currencySymbol + '&FarePrice=' + totalFares + '&ServicesPrice=' + totalServices + '&PNR=' + pnr + '&click_id=' + marketInSession;
            pixel.setAttribute('src', linkSource);
        }
    };
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    window.onload = function () {
        const pageEnum = {
            'Select': 'select',
            'Itinerary': 'itinerary'
        };
        const queryParameters = {
            'utm_content': '&utm_content=',
            'kayakclickid': '&kayakclickid='
        };
        const flows = {
            'BookingFlow': 'BOOKING_FLOW'
        };

        const perbookingCodesToAdd = ['SMS']

        const constants = {
            'decimals': 2
        };
		
		function isProductionEnviroment() {   
            var url = location.href;     
            return url.includes('pobeda.aero') && !url.includes('newshore.es');
        }
        
        const productionLinks = {
            'Aviasales': 'https://pixel.aviasales.ru',
            'Pobeda': 'https://tracker.pobeda.aero',
            'Kayack': 'https://www.kayak.com'
        };

        const testLinks = {
            'Aviasales': 'https://pixel.aviasalesTest.ru',
            'Pobeda': 'https://trackerTest.pobeda.aero',
            'Kayack': 'https://kayakpixeltest.com'
        };

        function pixelLinkRetriever(pixelName) {   
            return isProductionEnviroment()? productionLinks[pixelName] : testLinks[pixelName];
        }


        function shouldAddSSR(ssr) {
            return perbookingCodesToAdd.some(elem => elem === ssr);
        }

        function getValueFromString(sourceText, textToSearch, endSymbol) {
            var parameterValue = "";
            if (startIndex = sourceText.indexOf(textToSearch) !== -1) {
                startIndex = sourceText.indexOf(textToSearch);
                var substring = sourceText.substring(startIndex).replace(textToSearch, '');
                var endIndex = substring.indexOf(endSymbol);
                endIndex = endIndex != -1 ? endIndex : sourceText.length;
                parameterValue = substring.substring(0, endIndex);
            }
            return parameterValue;
        }

        
        function setMarketID(thereIsmarketInSession, url, parameterNameInQuery) {
            var queryHasParameter = parameterNameInQuery != '';
            if (url.includes(pageEnum.Select) && (queryHasParameter)) {
                var startIndex = url.indexOf(parameterNameInQuery);
                if (startIndex != -1) {
                    if (!queryHasParameter && thereIsmarketInSession) {
                        sessionStorage.removeItem('TrackerID')
                    } else {
                        var parameterValue = getValueFromString(url, parameterNameInQuery, '&')
                        sessionStorage.setItem('TrackerID', JSON.stringify({ trackerName: parameterNameInQuery, parameterValue: parameterValue }));
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        function getParameterNameInQuery(url) {
            var parameterNameInQuery = '';
            for (const parameter in queryParameters) {
                var parameterName = queryParameters[parameter];
                if (url.includes(parameterName)) {
                    parameterNameInQuery = parameterName;
                }
            }
            return parameterNameInQuery;
        }

        function getTicksDate() {
            var date = new Date();
            return (date.getTime() * 10000 + 621355968000000000);
        }

        function getTotalFares(booking) {
            var totalFares = 0;
            booking.journeys.forEach(journey => {
                journey.fares.forEach(fare => {
                    totalFares += parseFloat(fare.totalAmount);
                })
            });
            return totalFares;
        }

        function getTotalServices(booking) {
            var totalServices = 0;
            if (booking.pricing.breakdown.perPaxSegment != null && booking.pricing.breakdown.perPaxSegment != undefined) {
                booking.pricing.breakdown.perPaxSegment.forEach(service => {
                    totalServices += parseFloat(service.totalAmount);
                })
            }
            if (booking.pricing.breakdown.perBooking != null && booking.pricing.breakdown.perBooking != undefined) {
                booking.pricing.breakdown.perBooking.forEach(service => {
                    if (service.charges != null && service.charges != undefined) {
                        service.charges.forEach(charge => {
                            if (shouldAddSSR(charge.code)) {
                                totalServices += charge.amount;
                            }
                        })
                    }
                })
            }
            if (booking.pricing.breakdown.perPax != null && booking.pricing.breakdown.perPax != undefined) {
                booking.pricing.breakdown.perPax.forEach(service => {
                    totalServices += parseFloat(service.totalAmount);
                })
            }
            return totalServices;
        }

        function setCookieEmailTrackerPobeda() {
            var contacts = JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.getItem("DP-sessionData"))._value.session.booking.contacts[0].channels;
            var email = '';
            if (contacts != null && contacts != undefined && contacts != '') {
                contacts.forEach(contact => {
                    if (contact.type === 'Email') {
                        email = contact.info;
                    }
                })
            }
            document.cookie = 'EmailTracker=' + email + '; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT;path=/';
        }
		
        function setTrackerSessionID() {
            document.cookie = 'TrackerSessionID=' + create_UUID() + ';path=/';
        }

        function getTrackerSessionID() {
            return getValueFromString(document.cookie, 'TrackerSessionID=', ';')
        }
		
        function create_UUID() {
            var dt = new Date().getTime();
            var uuid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[x]/g, function (c) {
                var r = (dt + Math.random() * 16) % 16 | 0;
                dt = Math.floor(dt / 16);
                return (c == 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8)).toString(16);
            });
            return uuid;
        }

        var marketInSession = sessionStorage.getItem('TrackerID');
        var thereIsmarketInSession = marketInSession != '' && marketInSession != null && marketInSession != undefined;
        var url = location.href;
        if (url.includes(pageEnum.Itinerary)) {
            setCookieEmailTrackerPobeda();
        }

        var parameterNameInQuery = getParameterNameInQuery(url);
        setMarketID(thereIsmarketInSession, url, parameterNameInQuery);
        if (url.includes(pageEnum.Itinerary) && thereIsmarketInSession) {
            var booking = JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.getItem("DP-sessionData"))._value.session.booking;
            var pixel = document.getElementById('trackerPixelKayack');
            var pnr = booking.bookingInfo.recordLocator;
            var currencySymbol = booking.pricing.currency;
            var totalFares = getTotalFares(booking);
            var totalServices = getTotalServices(booking);
            marketInSession = JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.getItem("TrackerID")).parameterValue;
            parameterNameInQuery = JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.getItem("TrackerID")).trackerName;
            var linkSource = '';
            if (parameterNameInQuery === queryParameters.kayakclickid) {
                var flow = JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.getItem("DP-sessionData"))._value.session.flow;
                if (flow === flows.BookingFlow) {
                    var totalAmount = booking.pricing.totalAmount;
                    linkSource = pixelLinkRetriever('Kayack') + '/WidgetSearch.do?partner_code=pobeda&kayakclickid=' + marketInSession + '&price=' + totalAmount + '&currency=' + currencySymbol + '&confirmation=' + pnr + '&rand=' + getTicksDate();
                }
            };

            pixel.setAttribute('src', linkSource);

        }    
    };
</script>
<img id="trackerPixelKayack" style="display: none;"><script>
    dataLayer = [];
</script>
